					WHERE TCT.city_id = '8' AND TCT.city_deleted = '0' AND TCT.city_status = '1' AND TST.state_deleted = '0' AND TST.state_status = '1' AND TCN.country_deleted = '0' AND TCN.country_status = '1' ORDER BY TCT.city_name ASC, TST.state_name ASC, TCN.country_name ASC
